<Caramel> stream etiquette
<Caramel> Streaming is an integral part of Bronystate. In the past, we've had issues with people attention whoring in the chat and in general being a nuisance. I'm not saying this is an issue again, but we need to be careful about this. When someone is streaming, it is our responsibility to show the streamer the utmost respect. <pikorar> -_________- My whale is bigger.
